   window.fscUser = {id: 0, level: 0};
        window.adsEnabled = (function () {
            // disable adv for sponsored articles
            if (typeof ifq_article_no_adv !== 'undefined' && ifq_article_no_adv == true) {
                return false;
            }
            var retval = true;
            var cookieName = 'ifq-premium';
            var c = document.cookie.match('(^|;)\\s*' + cookieName + '\\s*=\\s*([^;]+)');
            // if cookie exists & value >= 1 then disable ads
            if (c && c.length > 1) {
                cval = c.pop();
                csplit = cval.split('%3A');
                if (csplit.length > 2) {
                    var mlevel = parseInt(csplit[2], 10);
                    if (csplit[2] == mlevel && (mlevel == 1 || mlevel == 2 || mlevel == 4 || mlevel == 8)) {
                        retval = false;
                    }
                    window.fscUser.level = mlevel;
                    window.fscUser.id = csplit[0];
                }
            }

            return retval;
        })();

function ifq_dfp_slot( slot_id, rightnow ) {
  var currentSlot = {
    prebid: null,
    dfp: null
  };

  var bidderTimeout = 5000;
  if (!ifq_dfp_slot.hasOwnProperty('slots')) {
    ifq_dfp_slot.slots = {};
  }
  if (!ifq_dfp_slot.hasOwnProperty('aps_slots')) {
    ifq_dfp_slot.aps_slots = [];
  }
  if (!ifq_dfp_slot.hasOwnProperty('no_aps_slots')) {
    ifq_dfp_slot.no_aps_slots = [];
  }
  if ( !ifq_dfp_slot.slots.hasOwnProperty(slot_id) ) {
    // slot has not already been defined
    ifq_dfp_slot.slots[slot_id] = null;
    try {
      var dataset = $('#' + slot_id).data();
      var slot_prefix = dataset['ownDfp'] ? '/132626232/' : '/150134580/';
      if (!('dfpNoPrefix' in dataset)) {
        slot_prefix += 'FATTOQDSK/';
      }
      var slot_name = dataset['adUnit'].startsWith('/') ? dataset['adUnit'] : slot_prefix + dataset['adUnit'];
      if (!(typeof window.adsEnabled === 'undefined' || window.adsEnabled) && !dataset['showAll']) {
        return;
      }
      if (dataset.hasOwnProperty('noIos') && (/iPad|iPhone|iPod/.test(navigator.userAgent) && !window.MSStream)) {
        return;
      }
      googletag.cmd.push(function() {
        var missingNetworks = ['prebid']; // ['prebid', 'aps'];

        function refreshSlot(network) {
          missingNetworks = missingNetworks.filter(function(item) {
              return item != network;
          });
          if (missingNetworks.length == 0) {
            var slot = ifq_dfp_slot.slots[slot_id];
            console.log("refreshing slot: ", currentSlot.dfp);
            googletag.pubads().refresh([slot]);
          }
        }

        currentSlot.dfp = {
          id: slot_id,
          unit: slot_name,
          size: dataset['sizes']
        };

        ifq_dfp_slot.slots[slot_id] = googletag.defineSlot(slot_name, dataset['sizes'], slot_id).addService(googletag.pubads());
        googletag.display(slot_id);

        var hasBidderSizes = ('apsSizes' in dataset && dataset['apsSizes'].length > 0);

        console.log("slot_id:", slot_id, "adUnit:", dataset['adUnit'], "hasBidderSizes:", hasBidderSizes, "apsSizes:", dataset['apsSizes']);

        if (!hasBidderSizes) {
          ifq_dfp_slot.no_aps_slots.push(ifq_dfp_slot.slots[slot_id]);
        }

        // TODO: set up sizes for prebid in bidderInfo or in div dataset
        if (dataset['adUnit'] in bidderInfo && hasBidderSizes) {
          currentSlot.prebid = {
            code: slot_id,
            mediaTypes: {
              banner: {
                sizes: dataset['apsSizes']
              }
            },
            bids: bidderInfo[dataset['adUnit']]
          };
        }

        /**
         * Ask prebid for bids (if appropriate)
         */
        if (currentSlot.prebid && (prebidInit === null || prebidInit)) {
          var prebidTimeout = setTimeout(function() {
            console.log("prebid timeout: refreshing slot");
            refreshSlot('prebid');
            prebidInit = false;
          }, bidderTimeout);

          pbjs.que.push(function() {
            pbjs.addAdUnits([currentSlot.prebid]);
            console.log("requesting prebids: ", currentSlot.prebid);
            pbjs.requestBids({
              bidsBackHandler: function() {
                prebidInit = true;
                // Clear timeout to avoid double GAM refresh
                if (prebidTimeout) {
                  console.log("clearing prebid timeout");
                  clearTimeout(prebidTimeout);
                }
                console.log("bids from prebid for", currentSlot.prebid);
                pbjs.setTargetingForGPTAsync([currentSlot.prebid.code]);
                refreshSlot('prebid');
                pbjs.removeAdUnit(currentSlot.prebid.code);
              },
              timeout: bidderTimeout
            });
          });
        } else { // some previous iteration of PB didn't complete succesfully, we should force a GAM refresh
          console.log("prebid no good or no units for prebid: refreshing GAM");
          console.log("prebidInit:", prebidInit);
          console.log("currentSlot:", currentSlot);
          refreshSlot('prebid');
        }

        if (dataset['parentClass']) {
          googletag.pubads().addEventListener('slotRenderEnded', function(event){
            if (slot_id == event.slot.getSlotElementId()) {
              if (!event.isEmpty) {
                $('#' + slot_id).parent().addClass(dataset['parentClass']);
              }
            }
          });
        }
        if (dataset['adUnit'] == 'FattoQ_Skin' && typeof ifqSkin == 'function' ) {
          googletag.pubads().addEventListener('slotRenderEnded', function(event){
            if (slot_id == event.slot.getSlotElementId()) {
              if (event.isEmpty) {
                console.log("[ADV] skin empty, calling fake skin");
                ifqSkin();
              }
            }
          });
        }
      });
    } catch (e) {
      console.error("problem with dfp slot " + slot_id + ": " + e);
    }
  } else {
    if (ifq_dfp_slot.slots[slot_id] != null) {
      // slot has already been defined _and_ populated, queue refresh
      try {
        googletag.pubads().refresh([ifq_dfp_slot.slots[slot_id]]);
      } catch (e) {
        console.error("problem refreshing dfp slot " + slot_id + ": " + e);
      }
    }
  }
}

function DFPinitPush() {
    googletag.cmd.push(function() {
        console.log('DFP started ************* ');
        googletag.pubads().collapseEmptyDivs();
        googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();
        googletag.pubads().disableInitialLoad();
        if (typeof window.ifq_section !== 'undefined') {
            googletag.pubads().setTargeting('section', ifq_section);
        }
                                if(window.gdprConsent === false){
            // only show non personalized ads if user deny consent
            console.log('DFP NON PERSONALIZED ADV only');
            googletag.pubads().setRequestNonPersonalizedAds(1);
        }
        googletag.enableServices();

        var dfpEvent = document.createEvent('Event');
        dfpEvent.initEvent('dfpinit', true, true);

        document.dispatchEvent(dfpEvent);

    });

    
    googletag.cmd.push(function() {
      var adunits = document.querySelectorAll("div.ifq-adv" );
      if(adunits.length > 0) {
        for (var i = 0; i < adunits.length; i++) {
          if (adunits[i].dataset.delayed && advDelayedObserver) {
            console.log("[ADV] delayed ad unit:", adunits[i].id);
            advDelayedObserver.observe(adunits[i]);
          } else {
            ifq_dfp_slot(adunits[i].id, true);
          }
        }
      } else {
        console.log("[ADV] No DfP slots found");
      }
    });

}

// Init DFP wether consent is granted or not (if not show non-personalized content)
if(typeof(window.gdprConsent) != 'undefined'){
    DFPinitPush();
}else{
   // show nothing and wait if consent gets granted
   // or wait for non personalized adv timeout (set in _build/dev/assets/js/async/head/gdpr.js)
   document.addEventListener('gdpr-initADV', DFPinitPush, false);
   document.addEventListener('gdpr-initNonPersonalizedADV', DFPinitPush, false);
}

       <h4>
        <script>
         var apiEndpoint = 'https://comments.ilfattoquotidiano.it';
        var encodedCurrentPath = encodeURIComponent(location.href);
            var shopEndpoint = 'https://shop.ilfattoquotidiano.it/ifq-gdpr-bridge';
        var logoutURL = 'https://shop.ilfattoquotidiano.it/logout/?location=' + encodedCurrentPath;
        var loginURL = 'https://shop.ilfattoquotidiano.it/login/';

        var localStorageExpire = 3600; // invalidate localStorage after this time in seconds
        //var ccManifest = ;
        var loadCommentScript = function (script, callback) {
            var scriptPath = 'https://www.ilfattoquotidiano.it/wp-content/themes/ifq-2019/assets/dist/custom-comments/' + script + '?ver=1616149057354';
            head.load([scriptPath], function () {
                callback();
            });
        }


        // set a custom event to allow notifications between different components in page
        var updateNotificationsBadge = document.createEvent('Event');
        updateNotificationsBadge.initEvent('updateNotificationsBadge', true, true);

        // if URL has hash, and this hash is "#settings", then open settings panel for current user
        var showSettingPanel = document.location.hash === '#settings';
        if (showSettingPanel)
			openSettingsPanel();



        function openSettingsPanel() {
            var userId = getUserId();
            var username = getUsername();
            openUserDetails(userId, null, true, username, 'settings');
        }
        // user details + settings in sidebar
    window.openUserDetails = function (userId, commenterId, showSettings, username, currentTab) {
        loadCommentScript('custom_comments_user_details.js', function(){
            // render in page
            var root = preact.render(preact.h(AuthorDetails, {
            baseClass: 'custom-comments-author-details',
            commenterId: commenterId,
            userId: parseInt(userId,10),
            showSettings: showSettings,
            currentTab: currentTab || 'comments',
            ownerName: username || getUsername(),
            username: username || getUsername(),
            apiEndpoint: apiEndpoint,
            shopEndpoint : shopEndpoint,
            localStorageExpire: localStorageExpire
            }), document.body);
        })
    }
        </script>
        <script>
         // INIT TOPBAR
        loadCommentScript('user_topbar.js', function () {
            renderUserTopBar();
            if(!window.ifq.load.isDefined('commenti-area-loaded')) {
                window.ifq.load('/wp-content/themes/ifq-2019/assets/dist/css/area/commenti-area.min.css?ver=1616149057354', 'commenti-area-loaded');
            }
        });

        function renderUserTopBar(additionalProps) {
            var wrapper = document.getElementById('top-bar-user');
            // we don't have the node to render, so exit (ie. on premium pages)
            if (!wrapper) {
                return;
            }

            // pass prop mobile:true if from mobile device
			var configObj =jQuery.extend({
				apiEndpoint: apiEndpoint,
                loginURL: loginURL,
                logoutURL: logoutURL,
                username: getUsername(),
                userId: getUserId(),
                userLevel : window.fscUser.level,
                pollingInterval: 60000, //check for new comments every [pollingInterval] ms
                maxIdleTime: 3600, // idle time in seconds: if there's no polling after this time reload entire thread
                localStorageExpire: localStorageExpire,
				mobile: false            }, additionalProps);

            wrapper.innerHTML = '';
            var root = preact.render(preact.h(TopBar, configObj), wrapper);
        }
        </script>
       </h4>

             </a>
            </picture>
           </div>
           <div class="container-text-primo-piano">
            <div class="catenaccio">
             <p>
             </p>
             <p>
              <a href="https://www.ilfattoquotidiano.it/2021/03/21/vaccinazioni-covid-ancora-caos-in-lombardia-per-mancato-invio-sms-a-cremona-asst-chiama-gli-aventi-diritto/6140591/">
               <span style="color: #8c0404;">
                <strong>
                 I VACCINI E LE REGIONI
                </strong>
               </span>
               – Continuano i problemi del sistema di prenotazioni (partecipata al 100% della Regione). A Cremona, come sabato, si presentano in 58 su 600 (
               <strong>
                leggi
               </strong>
               ).
              </a>
              <a href="https://www.ilfattoquotidiano.it/2021/03/21/vaccinazioni-caso-cremona-linfettivologa-balotta-che-isolo-il-virus-ora-e-anche-medico-volontario-inaccettabile-e-inconcepibile/6140815/">
               Balotta, infettivologa ex del Sacco e ora volontaria nell’ospedale cremonese: “Inconcepibile” (
               <strong>
                di G. Trinchella
               </strong>
               ).
              </a>
              <a href="https://www.ilfattoquotidiano.it/2021/03/21/lombardia-majorino-dopo-lennesimo-caso-aria-aspettiamo-nota-di-letizia-moratti-che-attacca-operato-di-letizia-moratti/6140605/">
               Le opposizioni contro la Regione: “Dirigenti inadeguati” (
               <strong>
                leggi
               </strong>
               )
              </a>
             </p>
            </div>

         <div data-vr-contentbox="">
          <h4 class="type-article">
           <a href="https://www.ilfattoquotidiano.it/diritti/">
            Diritti
           </a>
          </h4>
          <h2 class="main-title" data-vr-excerpttitle="">
           <span style="color: #8c0404;">
            <a href="https://www.ilfattoquotidiano.it/2021/03/21/omofobia-attivista-di-gaynet-aggredito-in-metropolitana-a-roma-calci-e-pugni-per-aver-dato-un-bacio-al-compagno/6140518/" style="color: #8c0404;">
             Coppia gay aggredita a Roma dopo un bacio.
            </a>
           </span>
           <a href="https://www.ilfattoquotidiano.it/2021/03/21/coppia-gay-aggredita-per-un-bacio-pd-e-m5s-parlamento-approvi-la-legge-contro-lomotransfobia-ma-la-lega-si-oppone/6140879/">
            Pd-M5s: “Ora legge contro l’omotransfobia”. Ma la Lega si oppone: “Strumentalizzano”
           </a>
          </h2>
          <div class="wrapper-all-primo-piano">
           <div class="container-main-data-primo-piano">
            <picture>

                 </a>
                </p>

                 <a href="https://www.ilfattoquotidiano.it/2021/03/21/regione-lombardia-e-rsa-lo-spi-cgil-temiamo-si-chiuda-tutto-con-uno-scambio-di-denaro-e-non-si-affrontino-i-problemi-veri/6136431/">
                  <strong>
                   <span style="color: #8c0404;">

                   </span>

         <div class="image-wrapper">
          <a aria-label="Mattarella: “Estirpare la mafia è possibile e necessario, iniziare con il rifiuto della compromissione”
" class="" href="https://www.ilfattoquotidiano.it/2021/03/21/mattarella-estirpare-la-mafia-e-possibile-e-necessario-rifiutare-compromissione-e-reticenza/6140516/">
           <img alt="" class="attachment-rullo img-landscape lazyload" data-src="https://st.ilfattoquotidiano.it/wp-content/uploads/2021/03/19/mattarella-330x173.jpg" height="173" loading="lazy" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" width="330"/>

         <div class="text-wrapper">
          <span class="argomento-item">
           <a href="https://www.ilfattoquotidiano.it/politica-palazzo/">
            Politica
           </a>
          </span>
          <h3 class="p-item">
           <a href="https://www.ilfattoquotidiano.it/2021/03/21/mattarella-estirpare-la-mafia-e-possibile-e-necessario-rifiutare-compromissione-e-reticenza/6140516/">
            Mattarella: “Estirpare la mafia è possibile e necessario, iniziare con il rifiuto della compromissione”
           </a>
          </h3>
          <!-- voci variabili -->
          <div class="correlati">
           <p>
            <a href="https://www.ilfattoquotidiano.it/2021/03/20/mafie-e-corruzione-vengono-spesso-da-una-politica-fiacca-e-un-po-complice-il-discorso-di-don-luigi-ciotti-per-il-21-marzo/6140390/">
             <strong>
              <span style="color: #8c0404;">
               DON CIOTTI –
              </span>
             </strong>
             Il messaggio: “Mafie e corruzione vengono spesso da una politica fiacca e un po’ complice” (di A. Corlazzoli)
            </a>
           </p>
           <p>
            <a href="https://www.ilfattoquotidiano.it/2021/03/20/giornata-per-le-vittime-di-mafia-libera-legge-i-nomi-al-cinema-palazzo-di-roma-unire-battaglia-contro-la-criminalita-alla-difesa-della-cultura/6140274/">
             <strong>
              <span style="color: #8c0404;">
               LA GIORNATA PER LE VITTIME –
              </span>
             </strong>
             A Roma la lettura dei nomi: “Unire battaglia per la legalità a quella per la cultura” (di A. Roma)
            </a>
           </p>
          </div>
         </div>

             Dottore di ricerca in diritto dell'economia
            </p>

            Diritti

          </span>
          <h3 class="p-item">
           <a href="https://www.ilfattoquotidiano.it/2021/03/21/anpi-dialogo-su-lavoro-e-costituzione-con-il-cardinale-di-bologna-matteo-zuppi-rivedi-lincontro/6140655/">
            Anpi, dialogo su Costituzione e lavoro con il cardinale di Bologna Zuppi. Rivedi l’incontro –
            <span style="color: #8c0404;">
             video
            </span>
           </a>
          </h3>

     <script>
      // -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    // INIT OUTBRAIN when global var initADV is set to true
    // or when global event gdpr-initADV GETS FIRED (defined in dev/assets/js/head/gdpr.js)
    // both check that advs are enabled (ie. user is not a partner/subscriber)
    // and that user has granted consent to gdpr
    var loadAsyncOutbrain = function(){
        // load when any element with the class widget_outbrain_widget comes into view
        var target = document.querySelector('div.widget_outbrain_widget');
        var loadOutbrain = function() {
            head.load('https://widgets.outbrain.com/outbrain.js', function(){
                console.log('ADV :: OUTBRAIN enabled *************** ');
            });
        }

        if(!target){
            loadOutbrain();
        } else {
            try {
                var lazyPolyfill = window.ifq.intersectionUrl;
                if(!window.ifq.load.isDefined('polyfill-loaded')) {
                    window.ifq.load(lazyPolyfill, 'polyfill-loaded');
                }
                window.ifq.load.ready('polyfill-loaded', function(){
                    var options = {
                        threshold: 0.4,
                    }
                    var outBrainLoaded = new IntersectionObserver(function(entries) {
                        entries.forEach(function(entry) {
                            if (entry.isIntersecting) {
                                loadOutbrain();
                                outBrainLoaded.unobserve(entry.target);
                            }
                        }, options)
                    });
                    ;
                    outBrainLoaded.observe(target);
                })
            } catch(e) {
                console.error("Problem loading outbrain:", e);
            }

        }
    }
    if(window.initADV){
        $('body').on('initComplete', function(){
            loadAsyncOutbrain();
        });
    } else {
        document.addEventListener('gdpr-initADV', loadAsyncOutbrain, false);
    }
    // -------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
     </script>
     <!-- endblock type: container-rulli -->

       <script>
        loadAsyncViralize = function() {
        window.vpt = window.vpt || {};
        window.vpt.queue = window.vpt.queue || [];
        window.vpt.queue.push(function () {
            window.vpt.on(window.vpt.EVENTS.ALL, function (evt) {
                console.log('[VPT] event:', evt);
            });
        });
        window.addEventListener('vptnoshow', function() {
            console.error('[VPT] no show');
        });

        var s = document.createElement("script");
        s.dataset.wid = 'auto';
        s.src = 'https://ads.viralize.tv/display/?zid=AAD2qw3QkMUS4g6B&enable_branding=0';
        document.body.appendChild(s);
    }

    if (window.initADV) {
        document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", loadAsyncViralize, false);
    } else {
        document.addEventListener('gdpr-initADV', loadAsyncViralize, false);
    }

  <script>
   function ifqSkin() {
            var $skyscraperWrap = document.querySelectorAll('.lateral-skyscraper');

            // check if we have enough lateral space
            var screenWidth = window.innerWidth || document.documentElement.clientWidth || document.body.clientWidth;
            var contentWidth = 1080;
            var hugeAdv = 300;
            var largeAdv = 160;
            var smallAdv = 120;
            var ad_width = 120;
            var availableSpace = (screenWidth - contentWidth) / 2;
            // if so, insert code into in-page placeholder
            if (availableSpace >= smallAdv) {
                if (availableSpace > hugeAdv) {
                    ad_width = hugeAdv;
                } else if (availableSpace > largeAdv) {
                    ad_width = largeAdv;
                }
                var unitSize = [ad_width, 600];
                if($skyscraperWrap && !!window.MSInputMethodContext && !!document.documentMode) {
                    var space =  document.querySelector('.sidebar').clientWidth;
                    var margin = (space - ad_width);
                    var $left_adv = document.querySelector('.lateral-skyscraper-left');
                    var $right_adv = document.querySelector('.lateral-skyscraper-right');
                    $left_adv.style.left = margin+'px';
                    $right_adv.style.right =margin+'px';
                    $left_adv.style.top =  (window.innerHeight / 4)+'px';
                    $right_adv.style.top = window.innerHeight / 4  +'px';
                }
                var $left_adv = document.querySelector('.lateral-skyscraper-left');
                var $right_adv = document.querySelector('.lateral-skyscraper-right');
                $left_adv.style.width = ad_width+'px';
                $right_adv.style.width = ad_width+'px';

                // ga('send', 'event', 'ifq_skin', 'showing-' + ad_width);
                var fake_skin = {
                    'fake-skin-sx': {'adUnit': 'FattoQ_FakeSkin_sx'},
                    'fake-skin-dx': {'adUnit': 'FattoQ_FakeSkin_dx'}
                }
               if (window.adsEnabled) {

                    googletag.cmd.push(function () {
                        for (var slot_id in fake_skin) {
                            var fakeSkinDiv = document.getElementById(slot_id);
                            fakeSkinDiv.dataset.sizes = JSON.stringify(unitSize);
                            fakeSkinDiv.dataset.apsSizes = JSON.stringify(unitSize);
                            fakeSkinDiv.dataset.adUnit = fake_skin[slot_id]['adUnit'];
                            console.log(fakeSkinDiv);
                            ifq_dfp_slot(slot_id, true);
                        }
                    });
             }
            }
        }
        if (typeof 'window.ifqShowSkin' !== 'undefined' && window.ifqShowSkin) {
            ifqSkin();
        }
  </script>

  <script>
   function displayFloorAd() {
        var fallbackDone = false;

        window.removeEventListener('scroll', displayFloorAd);

        function filterApsSizes(sizes) {
            var apsSizes = ["[300,50]","[320,50]","[320,100]","[300,250]","[336,280]","[300,600]","[728,90]","[970,90]","[970,250]","[160,600]"];
            return sizes.filter(function(size) {
                var s = JSON.stringify(size);
                return (apsSizes.indexOf(s) > -1);
            });
        }

        var fallbackAdUnit = '/22141773216,22265506341/ilfattoquotidiano.it_floorad_dsk';

        var adUnit = head.mobile ? 'ilfattoquotidiano_floorad_mobile-erogazione': 'FattoQ_FloorAd_Erogazione';

        googletag.cmd.push(function() {
            var clientWidth = document.body.clientWidth;
            var sizes, divHeight, divWidth;

            if (!head.mobile) {
                if (clientWidth > 728) {
                    sizes = [[728,90],[2,5]];
                    divHeight = 90;
                    divWidth = 728;
                }
                if (clientWidth > 970) {
                    sizes.push([970,250]);
                    divHeight = 250;
                    divWidth = 970;
                }
            } else {
                sizes = [[300, 50],[300, 100],[320, 50],[320, 100]];
                divHeight = 100;
                divWidth = 320;
            }

            var apsSizes = JSON.stringify(filterApsSizes(sizes));
            sizes = JSON.stringify(sizes);

            var divId = 'div-gpt-ad-floor' + (head.mobile ? 'mobile' : '');
            var div = document.createElement('div');
            div.style.position = 'fixed';
            if (head.mobile) {
                div.style.width = '100%';
            } else {
                div.style.minWidth = (divWidth + 20) + 'px';
                div.style.borderColor = 'rgba(50, 50, 50, 0.5)';
            }
            div.style.maxHeight = divHeight + 2 + 'px';
            div.style.left = 0;

            div.style.zIndex = 2000000;
            var $socialAB = document.querySelector('.social-ab-fixed');
            if(!$socialAB) {
                div.style.bottom = 0;
            } else {
                div.classList.add('floor-adv');
            }
            var intermediate_div = document.createElement('div');
            intermediate_div.style.position = 'relative';
            intermediate_div.style.margin = '0px auto';
            intermediate_div.style.width = divWidth + 'px';
            intermediate_div.style.height = divHeight + 'px';
            intermediate_div.style.backgroundColor = 'transparent';
            div.appendChild(intermediate_div);

            var innerDiv = document.createElement('div');
            innerDiv.id = divId;
            innerDiv.style.position = 'absolute';
            innerDiv.style.bottom = '0px';
            innerDiv.dataset.adUnit = adUnit;
            innerDiv.dataset.sizes = sizes;
            // Only on mobile
            innerDiv.dataset.apsSizes = apsSizes;
            intermediate_div.appendChild(innerDiv);

            var closer = document.createElement('a');
            closer.id = 'mvup-floorad-closer';
            closer.setAttribute('style', 'display: block; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; border-radius: 0px; border: 0px; min-width: 0px; min-height: 0px; width: 20px; height: 20px; max-width: 20px; max-height: 20px; position: absolute; 0px 0px no-repeat; z-index: 2000012; opacity: 0.8; top: -20px; right: 0px; cursor: pointer');
            closer.style.background = 'url("data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAABQAAAAUBAMAAAB/pwA+AAAAElBMVEX///8bGxve3t4jIyOfn58AAABFp2ARAAAABXRSTlOZ76HqtCBGSRoAAABBSURBVAjXYyAMWIxApLIDkGAOVGBgYBI1YACRQgwMiiA+mAJzIcJgQYgwSBAqDBNEMBEKENoQhqFagbAY4RyCAAD8DwlN+MjxmgAAAABJRU5ErkJggg==")';
            closer.addEventListener('click', function() { div.remove() });
            var n = intermediate_div.appendChild(closer);

            document.body.appendChild(div);
            ifq_dfp_slot(divId, true);

            // add slot render ended prendendo event.size
            googletag.pubads().addEventListener('slotRenderEnded', function(event) {
                if (divId == event.slot.getSlotElementId()) {
                    if (event.isEmpty) {
                        if (!fallbackDone && !head.mobile) {
                            if (adUnit == fallbackAdUnit) {
                                console.log("[floor ad] - don't fallback to same unit");
                                return;
                            }
                            fallbackDone = true;
                            divId = divId + '-fallback';
                            innerDiv.remove();
                            console.log("[floorad] fallback to ad unit", fallbackAdUnit);
                            var fallbackDiv = document.createElement('div');
                            fallbackDiv.id = divId;
                            fallbackDiv.style.position = 'absolute';
                            fallbackDiv.style.bottom = '0px';
                            fallbackDiv.dataset.adUnit = fallbackAdUnit;
                            fallbackDiv.dataset.sizes = sizes;
                            fallbackDiv.dataset.apsSizes = apsSizes;
                            div.appendChild(fallbackDiv);
                            ifq_dfp_slot(divId, true);
                        } else {
                            console.log("[floorad] closing empty ad:", event);
                            div.remove();
                        }
                    } else {
                        try {
                            console.log("[floorad] setting height following event:", event);
                            var h =  innerDiv.offsetHeight;
                            var w = innerDiv.offsetWidth;
                            console.log("h:", h, "w:", w);
                            if (event.size[0] == 2 && event.size[1] == 5) {
                                console.log("[floorad] size 2x5 - hiding div");
                                div.style.display = 'none';
                            } else {
                                div.style.backgroundColor = 'rgba(60, 60, 60, 0.5)';
                                if (h > 1 && w > 1) {  // to avoid resizing to [1,1], which we sometime get both with event.size and measuring the div
                                    div.style.height = innerDiv.offsetHeight + 'px';
                                    intermediate_div.style.width = innerDiv.offsetWidth  + 'px';
                                    intermediate_div.style.height = innerDiv.offsetHeight + 'px';
                                }
                            }
                        } catch(err) {
                            console.error("[floorad] error while getting size:", event.size, err);
                        }
                    }
                }
            });
        });
    }

    if (head.mobile) {
        window.addEventListener('dfpinit', displayFloorAd);
    } else {
        window.addEventListener('scroll', displayFloorAd);
    }
  </script>
